        <div class="aspect" style="padding-top:61.42578125%;"></div>
    </div>
        </a>
    </div>
            </div>    
        
        
        <h1 class="excerpt-title">
            <span class="">
                <a href="https://www.voiceofsandiego.org/topics/government/civic-san-diego-chief-paid-leave-following-retirement-announcement/">Civic San Diego Chief on Paid Leave Following Retirement Announcement</a>
            </span>
        </h1>
        <div class="excerpt-byline">
                    
    <div class="vo-byline -author ">
                    <cite class="">
                <a href="https://www.voiceofsandiego.org/author/lisa-halverstadt/">Lisa Halverstadt</a><span class="delim"></span>            </cite>
                <div class="article-meta">
                                <a class="vo-post-time" href="https://www.voiceofsandiego.org/topics/government/civic-san-diego-chief-paid-leave-following-retirement-announcement/">
                    <time>March 16, 2018</time>
            </a>
                                </div>
    </div>
        </div>
        <div class="excerpt-lede">
            <p>Embattled Civic president Reese Jarrett, who abruptly announced plans to retire last month amid increasing controversy, is not expected to return to work.</p>

        </div>

            <div class="excerpt-post-tag">
                
    <div class="vo-post-tag  -cat-land-use  ">

        <h1 class="excerpt-title">
            <a href="https://www.voiceofsandiego.org/topics/news/san-diego-explained-port-undertaking-biggest-arts-project-yet/">San Diego Explained: The Port is Undertaking Its Biggest Arts Project Yet</a>
        </h1>    
        <div class="excerpt-lede">
            <p>On this week’s episode, Voice of San Diego’s Kinsee Morlan and NBC 7’s Monica Dean consider the Port of San Diego’s public arts program.</p>

        </div>
        <div class="excerpt-byline">
                <a class="vo-post-time" href="https://www.voiceofsandiego.org/topics/news/san-diego-explained-port-undertaking-biggest-arts-project-yet/">
                    <time>March 15, 2018</time>
            </a>
        </div>
    </div>
                    </div>

    <div class="vo-thumb -video " 
        data-module="thumb-video"

        data-video-id=""
        data-popup="false">

        <a href="https://www.voiceofsandiego.org/topics/news/san-diego-explained-dockless-bikes-everywhere/">
                

    
    <div class="vo-thumb -bg " 
        data-module="thumb"
        data-retina=""
